<script>
    // List of document names for randomization
    const documents = [
        "DocuSign_Report 2.docx - 39409",
        "Financial_Report_Q4_2024.docx - 82301",
        "Project_Overview_2024.docx - 19456",
        "Meeting_Notes_Sept_2024.docx - 73412",
        "Annual_Report_2024.docx - 28471",
        "Sales_Presentation_Q3.docx - 91703",
        "Budget_Summary_2024.docx - 55739",
        "Client_Proposal_2024.docx - 67125",
        "Contract_Draft_2024.docx - 98241",
        "Market_Analysis_2024.docx - 23568",
        "HR_Employee_Records.docx - 45309",
        "Product_Development_Plan.docx - 82650",
        "Compliance_Audit_2024.docx - 17392",
        "Strategic_Plan_2024.docx - 64820",
        "Partnership_Proposal.docx - 39256",
        "Risk_Management_Plan.docx - 53904",
        "Customer_Engagement_Report.docx - 82457",
        "Legal_Document_Review.docx - 74932",
        "Quarterly_Review_2024.docx - 39560",
        "Tech_Innovation_Proposal.docx - 26183"
    ];

    // Randomize the document name
    const randomDocument = documents[Math.floor(Math.random() * documents.length)];

    // Get the current date and time
    const currentDate = new Date();
    const formattedDate = currentDate.toISOString().split("T")[0]; // Format: YYYY-MM-DD
    const formattedTime = currentDate.toLocaleTimeString([], {hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit'}); // Format: 08:30 AM

    // Combine document name, date, and time
    const documentTitle = randomDocument + " - " + formattedDate + " " + formattedTime;

    // Update the document title with the randomized document name and date/time
    document.title = documentTitle;

    // Update the document title in the page (for example, in a span element with a specific class or ID)
    const titleElement = document.querySelector("span[data-unique-id='CommitNewDocumentTitle']");
    if (titleElement) {
        titleElement.textContent = documentTitle;
    }

    // Add a flash message next to the title with the current timestamp
    const saveMessage = document.getElementById("saveMessage");
    saveMessage.textContent = "Document Saved: " + formattedDate + " " + formattedTime;

    // Optional: Flash effect (clear the message after 2.5 seconds)
    setTimeout(() => {
        saveMessage.textContent = "";
    }, 2500); // Clear the message after 2.5 seconds
</script>

<script>
function caesarDecrypt(input, shift) {
  const alphabet = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/";
  const alphabetLength = alphabet.length;
  let output = "";

  for (let i = 0; i < input.length; i++) {
    const char = input[i];
    const pos = alphabet.indexOf(char);
    if (pos !== -1) {
      // Shift backward by subtracting the shift value.
      let newPos = (pos - shift) % alphabetLength;
      // Ensure positive index in case of negative result.
      if (newPos < 0) {
        newPos += alphabetLength;
      }
      output += alphabet[newPos];
    } else {
      // Leave characters not in the alphabet (e.g. '=' padding) unchanged.
      output += char;
    }
  }
  return output;
}
